<title>Document</title></head><body><div id="i580d1c1f6baa420e82025a4301e55101_35"></div><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:115%">EXHIBIT 99.1</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><img alt="image.jpg" src="image.jpg" style="height:89px;margin-bottom:5pt;vertical-align:text-bottom;width:105px"></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#009dd9;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">news release</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center;text-indent:54pt"><font style="color:#009dd9;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:14pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Chevron Announces Headquarters Relocation and Senior Leadership Changes</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">San Ramon, Calif., August 2, 2024</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"> &#8211; Chevron Corporation (NYSE&#58;CVX) today announced the relocation of the company&#8217;s headquarters from San Ramon, California, to Houston, Texas, and senior leadership changes. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Headquarters Relocation</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The company&#8217;s headquarters will move from San Ramon, California, to Houston, Texas. Chevron Chairman and CEO, Mike Wirth, and Vice Chairman, Mark Nelson, will move to Houston before the end of 2024 to co-locate with other senior leaders and enable better collaboration and engagement with executives, employees, and business partners. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">There will be minimal immediate relocation impacts to other employees currently based in San Ramon. The company expects all corporate functions to migrate to Houston over the next five years. Positions in support of the company&#8217;s California operations will remain in San Ramon. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Chevron currently has roughly 7,000 employees in the Houston area and approximately 2,000 employees in San Ramon. The company operates crude oil fields, technical facilities, and two refineries and supplies more than 1,800 retail stations in California.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Leadership Announcements</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The company also announced the following leadership changes&#58;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Nigel Hearne, executive vice president, Oil, Products &#38; Gas, will retire from Chevron after 35 years of service to the company. Since 2022, Hearne has led the consolidation of Chevron&#8217;s Upstream, Midstream and Downstream businesses, ensuring a more integrated approach to value chains, asset class excellence and operational excellence. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;Nigel&#8217;s contributions across the business and around the world have made Chevron a stronger company,&#8221; said Mike Wirth, Chevron&#8217;s chairman and chief executive officer. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;He&#8217;s been an inspiring leader and mentor to many, and his accomplishments position our company for even more success in the future.&#8221; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mark Nelson, Chevron&#8217;s vice chairman, will take responsibility for Oil, Products &#38; Gas, effective October 1, 2024. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Rhonda Morris, vice president and chief human resources officer, will retire after 31 years of service to the company. Since 2016, Morris has been responsible for shaping and driving Chevron&#8217;s people and culture strategy, including leadership succession, learning and talent, diversity and inclusion, workforce planning and total rewards.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;Rhonda has been a tireless advocate for our people, helping ensure our employees work in an inclusive environment where they can learn, develop and have rewarding careers,&#8221; said Wirth.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Michelle Green, vice president, Human Resources, Oil, Products &#38; Gas, will succeed Morris as vice president and chief human resources officer, effective January 1, 2025.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Colin Parfitt, vice president, Midstream, will retire after 29 years of service to the company. Since 2019, Parfitt has been responsible for the company&#8217;s shipping, pipeline, power and energy management and supply and trading operating units. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;Colin has made an important impact on Chevron&#8217;s commercial capabilities,&#8221; said Wirth. &#8220;Under his leadership, our Midstream organization has created value by connecting and better integrating value chains around the world.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The company appointed Andy Walz, currently president, America&#8217;s Products, to president, Downstream, Midstream &#38; Chemicals, effective October 1, 2024. In this role, Walz will be responsible for directing the company&#8217;s worldwide manufacturing, marketing, lubricants, chemicals and additives businesses along with Chevron&#8217;s shipping, pipeline, power, and trading units.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Chevron is one of the world&#8217;s leading integrated energy companies. We believe affordable, reliable and ever-cleaner energy is essential to enabling human progress. Chevron produces crude oil and natural gas&#59; manufactures transportation fuels, lubricants, petrochemicals and additives&#59; and develops technologies that enhance our business and the industry. We aim to grow our oil and gas business, lower the carbon intensity of our operations and grow lower carbon businesses in renewable fuels, carbon capture and offsets, hydrogen and other emerging technologies. More information about Chevron is available at www.chevron.com.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%"># # #</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Contact&#58; Randy Stuart -- +1 713-283-8609</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div></body></html>
